< review>
Item: Bespoke Tailcoat Tuxedo (for my wedding)
Tailor: Jerry B.

Timeliness: 5/5
Service: 5/5
Quality: 5/5
Accessibility: 4/5 (parking can be tricky, product can be pricey)

Getting married has always been one of the most important life events in my eyes, so I wanted to make sure that what I wore really reflected that.  I opted for a "bespoke" (custom-made) tailcoat tuxedo, with a unique and uncommon cut that really drew my eye, and contacted quite a few tailors around Los Angeles and Orange County to see if they would be able to pull it off in time for my wedding.  Looking at examples and testimonials, JB had been my first choice from the start--so when I heard back from Jerry that they would be able to accommodate me, I was thrilled.  I sent over the closest image I could find to what I was picturing, and we scheduled a meeting.

My first visit, we discussed every aspect of the suit, from the cuts and designs of each piece, to the actual style and type of fabric.  He was very thorough, and gave great personal recommendations for different options.  Jerry then did just about every type of measurement I could imagine, and triple-checked every single one to make sure everything was precise.  When we finished up, I had a really good feeling about it all, and left everything in his hands.

The second visit (about a month later), I went in to do a fitting of the now fully-made tailcoat--again, a fantastic experience (Jerry and Angelo are just really great people).  The suit looked very good at that point, I would say 90/100 at that very first fitting.  But pro-tip: don't stress about the first fitting, it is the fine-tuning afterward that really makes the biggest difference.  Jerry is a perfectionist, so he made some marks to take in small bits here and there, and said they'd have it ready for a final fitting within a few days.

I just went in today for the final fitting, and the difference was really pretty incredible...those last few alterations of his absolutely took it to 100/100 for me.  Not only is the style spot on with what I had imagined / referenced, but it fits like a glove--easily the most comfortable outfit I own at this point, and it's a 3-piece suit lol.  Jerry has a real eye for this stuff, and seeing it all come together, his suggestions are on point, and come from experience in the industry.

Bottom line: I couldn't be happier with my choice.  Jerry is a tremendous talent, and he and Angelo made every step of the process easy for me.
It's expensive, for sure, but coming from someone NOT rolling in dough, it was absolutely worth it.  At the end of the day, it's an investment in yourself.  There are going to be some really big, important moments in your life, and you deserve to look and feel like a million bucks in those moments, in every way--and that's exactly what these guys do.

***Pictures to come after the wedding***<//review>

<Date>1617329745973</Date><Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
I love to go thrifting! Who doesn't???
That said there are things I love about this location. Let's start with the clothes because that's why I usually go there. They color code so the shoulder of the garment will have a colored plastic that may or may not correlate to extra savings that day so ask what the color of the day is for tour 50% discount. The clothes are all clean. I believe they wash everything. Unless its "new" w tags. The problem. Witb this method is they ruin all the sweaters that should be dry cleaned so this isn't the place you will find any good wool or cashmere. I did score a great Prada sweater one day with all the tags inside and I de pilled it and stitched a 1/4 inch seam and I get so many compliments. $4 dollars on 50% off.
So of you have lots of time to comb through stuff this could be a spit for the occasional "score"
They make a couple huge errors in my opinion. In how they display. Its good that they put all the items by category and color family however. I would love to see them take the extra step and sprite by size. I almost want to do it myself and say just trade my time for some clothes lol. I mean you will get fatigued when you see something cute and it's too big or too small. And they put stuff out that can have major damage so CHECK EVERY SINGLE PIECE. I grabbed 2 dresses only to find one looked like it had been used for rifle practice the holes at the bottom were so big I made them take it off the floor. And then the other the bottom hem was shot all fraying and not meant to be. So again CHECK EVERY PIECE.
They have generally good pricing on clothes sometimes they have a special red tag price and it can often be too much because they think it's designer and its VENUS or Old Navy. So be observant.
They have a small room for home goods that are "curated" and I see some things but they are VERY overpriced. This is the main reason I can not give 5 stars.
They have racks of glass and plastic and wood home stuff and well you other thrift type things.
This is about a medium sized place not big so it won't make you too crazy time wise to see just about everything. The staff here is great!! So friendly and surprisingly helpful. For a thrift store. And as always they Salvation Army helps people in need so its a give back type of experience.
Today I got some fun pieces a hot pink sweater. So cute and trendy and a GORGEOUS Sundance eyelet top perfect for summer and a couple other little things. One was I thought a nude colored pleated skirt but turns out its gauchos so that will get donated. And then a cute cropped gap bathing sweater. You will enjoy this shop. I take my hand sanitizer and dig!!
I hope you love it as much as me. ‚ù§<//review>

< text>
Wow, I've really never had thalis before and came here because I saw great Yelp reviews and I wasn't disappointed! I came here at around 8 pm on a Wednesday night and didn't have to wait at all and was seated in a group of 7 at a nice table in the back.

Food: I got the first thali option with the unlimited option. It was actually a huge amount of food and I basically didn't need to get second helpings. I loved that they gave us roti to dip all of the sauces and food in and it was really a good amount of food! I was terribly full afterwards but super super happy. I haven't had much Southern Indian food before so it added to the experience and I really did like the way that it was so family style.

Service: There's not many people helping out in the restaurant but they came by fairly often to check in on us and make sure that we had all of the food and that we got second helpings.

Ambiance: Super casual and kind of run down venue, but it feels very homey and very kitchen-esque.

Overall loved the unique food experience and would come again! Super cheap and affordable too.< /text>

< Text>
Authentic South Indian meals, but chaotic management.

I ordered the (unlimited) lunch Thali, and this was hands down the *most authentic* South Indian food I‚Äôve had in the US. The food tasted exactly like how my mom makes it! I cannot stress how thrilled I was to find that even the yogurt is home-made from Indian yogurt cultures ‚Äî I have not seen any other restaurant serve Indian yogurt. üòÉ

(Like some reviewers mentioned, I don‚Äôt think any of the staff is South Indian. How ironic then that the food is so superlative.)

Unfortunately, they seem ill-equipped to handle large crowds. Like other reviews mention, there is no clear greeting for patrons entering the restaurant, there is no waiting area, my food took 30 minutes to arrive, some items were missing from my plate, and I had to ask several times before they were delivered. The staff tried to be friendly and helpful, but they seemed overwhelmed.

It breaks my heart that a restaurant with such good food has to garner poor reviews because of its management. I hope they re-think their management system soon.

-2 stars for the chaos, +1 star for exceptionally good food.</Text>

The Thali was simply superb - very much like home cooked food - the kind of food that brings back fond memories. The variety was great, the flavors of individual thali items were top notch, nothing was too oily. The service was super quick and the servers polite and attentive as well.

All in all, we had a great wholesome and authentic lunch. Will highly recommend this gem of a restaurant!<//review>

< time>
1556509142283</time>
<rating>4<//rating>< text>
Ugadi marks the beginning of the new Hindu lunar calendar. It is a time of celebration for the Telugu and Kannada communities during which special vegetarian dishes are made and served to family and friends.

If this restaurant was based on that premises then food definitely resonates with the vibe. The flavors are great and the menu also contains standard South Indian dishes. I have been here a few times and tasted multiple dishes and I think it is time to write a review.

The ‚ÄúBhojanam‚Äù thali is a must have. Good varieties of vegetables are served with Sambar and Rasam. The majjiga (buttermilk) is however served in plastic cups which I felt was a bit disappointing from a presentation standpoint but it works. The desert that is served with the thali could be a bit better that a laddu.

The idly, dosas and other snacks are above standard and you will definitely leave the restaurant satisfied.

However a couple of things can take this restaurant from being good to amazing like: increase staff during weekends, they seem to be just managing somehow during the peak hours. They seem to be unorganized when the place is busy. The look and feel of the place can be improved and enhanced to resemble the festival of Ugadi. Otherwise i would say that the food is definitely a must try for all hardcore South Indian vegetarians out there.<//text>

<user_id>111555979736888115248<//user_id><name>Akhilesh Shirbhate< /name><Date>1552457549590< /Date><rating>5</rating><Text>The food was very good. Homely taste. The restaurant was run by elderly people - orders, management, billing, serving. They were lovely to talk to. The food itself was very tasty and fresh. The chapati were cooked fresh and has the distinct aroma of home-made fulkas. The quantity was  unlimited as I ordered the "bhojanam" (unlimited thali. It has quite a variety of dishes - 2 vegetable curries, daal, rasam, sweet, curd, rice, fulkas, etc. The unlimited thali at $11.99 was well worth it. We also ordered an idly sambar and mango lassi. Idly sambar was very flavorful. The mango lassi was the best I had over last few years. Overall, the place is a hidden gem!</Text>< Pictures>

<review>If you‚Äôre lazy to cook, but want to eat something healthy, vegetarian, tasty and homemade-like, go to Ugadi.

Food: This place offers variety of Andhra tiffins apart from Thali. Their unlimited Thali includes curry/poriyal, dal, sambar, rasam, curry to go with bread, sweet, curd, buttermilk, fryms and your choice of bread (poori/phulka). Ugadi is one of those few places which serve authentic phulkas.

Service: Staff is very friendly, especially an older lady who sits near the cash counter (must be owner or a relative of owner). She personally goes to every table to check on customers.

Ambience: It‚Äôs a small place, and usually not crowded.

Price: Food is reasonably priced. I would give a $.<//review>< pictures>

< text>
Excellent home-style andhra food in a casual setting. Service has been friendly and quick every time I've been there, and they will also pack their thali to go (resulting in an impressive array of small boxes) which a lot of thali places don't seem to like to do. If you are really hungry, though, you should eat in because the thali is pretty much unlimited for any of the items that they serve -- just tell them what you'd like to have more of.

For any neophytes reading this, be aware that food from Andhra Pradesh tends to be quite spicy and "home-style" means that you might encounter dishes that you don't tend to run into on a menu in most Indian restaurants, such as karela (or kakarakaya in Telugu) which is a bitter, spiny vegetable that can fall into the "love it or hate it" category for a lot of people. If you are a little less adventurous, you may want to order specific items from the menu instead of the thali which comes as a tray (thali) of a lot of little dishes of various vegetable or dal preparations.<//text>

< Text>
This review is for thali only

Visited for lunch on Sunday.
After going inside, there was nobody at the register to take the order. Waited for very long for someone to take my order.
Buttermilk was delicious with ginger and cilantro in it.
Appetizer vada with ginger chutney was ok. They removed 'masala' from the masala vada. Attached photo.
Waited for another 20 min to get the thali.
Roti ------  cold and bad. Just tasted and left it aside.
Spinach Daal - Bland
Gongura pickle -- Ok
Rasam -- Average
Sambar  -- ok
Dessert Gulab jamun was average.

P.S. In short, all the curries in the thali were bland without any salt or spices. This type of curries are served for old people back in India, when doctor warned them to cut down on spices...!!</Text>
